\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01287}01287\ \textcolor{comment}{\ Introduction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01288}01288\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01289}01289\ \textcolor{comment}{\ sal.h\ provides\ a\ set\ of\ annotations\ to\ describe\ how\ a\ function\ uses\ its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01290}01290\ \textcolor{comment}{\ parameters\ -\/\ the\ assumptions\ it\ makes\ about\ them,\ and\ the\ guarantees\ it\ makes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01291}01291\ \textcolor{comment}{\ upon\ finishing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01292}01292\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01293}01293\ \textcolor{comment}{\ Annotations\ may\ be\ placed\ before\ either\ a\ function\ parameter's\ type\ or\ its\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01294}01294\ \textcolor{comment}{\ type,\ and\ describe\ the\ function's\ behavior\ regarding\ the\ parameter\ or\ return\ value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01295}01295\ \textcolor{comment}{\ There\ are\ two\ classes\ of\ annotations:\ buffer\ annotations\ and\ advanced\ annotations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01296}01296\ \textcolor{comment}{\ Buffer\ annotations\ describe\ how\ functions\ use\ their\ pointer\ parameters,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01297}01297\ \textcolor{comment}{\ advanced\ annotations\ either\ describe\ complex/unusual\ buffer\ behavior,\ or\ provide}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01298}01298\ \textcolor{comment}{\ additional\ information\ about\ a\ parameter\ that\ is\ not\ otherwise\ expressible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01299}01299\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01300}01300\ \textcolor{comment}{\ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01301}01301\ \textcolor{comment}{\ Buffer\ Annotations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01302}01302\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01303}01303\ \textcolor{comment}{\ The\ most\ important\ annotations\ in\ sal.h\ provide\ a\ consistent\ way\ to\ annotate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01304}01304\ \textcolor{comment}{\ buffer\ parameters\ or\ return\ values\ for\ a\ function.\ Each\ of\ these\ annotations\ describes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01305}01305\ \textcolor{comment}{\ a\ single\ buffer\ (which\ could\ be\ a\ string,\ a\ fixed-\/length\ or\ variable-\/length\ array,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01306}01306\ \textcolor{comment}{\ or\ just\ a\ pointer)\ that\ the\ function\ interacts\ with:\ where\ it\ is,\ how\ large\ it\ is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01307}01307\ \textcolor{comment}{\ how\ much\ is\ initialized,\ and\ what\ the\ function\ does\ with\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01308}01308\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01309}01309\ \textcolor{comment}{\ The\ appropriate\ macro\ for\ a\ given\ buffer\ can\ be\ constructed\ using\ the\ table\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01310}01310\ \textcolor{comment}{\ Just\ pick\ the\ appropriate\ values\ from\ each\ category,\ and\ combine\ them\ together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01311}01311\ \textcolor{comment}{\ with\ a\ leading\ underscore.\ Some\ combinations\ of\ values\ do\ not\ make\ sense\ as\ buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01312}01312\ \textcolor{comment}{\ annotations.\ Only\ meaningful\ annotations\ can\ be\ added\ to\ your\ code;\ for\ a\ list\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01313}01313\ \textcolor{comment}{\ these,\ see\ the\ buffer\ annotation\ definitions\ section.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01314}01314\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sal_8h_source_l01315}01315\ \textcolor{comment}{\ Only\ a\ single\ buffer\ annotation\ should\ be\ used\ for\ each\ parameter.}}
